method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)

  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)

    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];

    i := i + 1;

  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y

  var b' := b + [y];

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
  assert ValidSolution(a, b);
}

The original program (without assertions) is:

```dafny
ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

  var b' := b + [y];

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
    decreases |a| - i
  {

      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      assert DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0;
      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {

      assert DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i];
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      // Append a[i + 1] to b such that the dot product with a[..i] stays zero.
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);
      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
      // After this step, i is even and the invariant still holds.
    } else {
      // Append -a[i - 1] to b for the odd case.
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);
      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);
      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a, b) == DotProduct(a'[..|a'|-1], b'[..|b'|-1]);
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a'[..|a'|-1], b'[..|b'|-1]) + a'[*] * b'[*];
  assert a'[*] == x;
  assert b'[*] == y;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  // The following proof is straightforward by definition of DotProduct
  // but we provide an explicit proof via rewriting.
  // Let a' = a + [x], b' = b + [y].
  // Then |a'| = |a| + 1 = |b| + 1 = |b'|.
  // By definition of DotProduct:
  // DotProduct(a', b') = DotProduct(a, b) + a'[-1] * b'[-1] = DotProduct(a, b) + x * y.
  // This matches the desired result.
  // No additional assertions needed.
  assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // After loop completion, |b| == |a| and i == |a|.
  // We need to show that DotProduct(a, b) == 0.
  // From the invariant for i == |a| (which is even because |a| is even),
  // we have DotProduct(a[..|a|], b) == 0, i.e. DotProduct(a, b) == 0.
  assert DotProduct(a, b) == 0;

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

}

  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y; // lemma proof
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)

    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]

      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      assert AllBounded(b, 100);

    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      // Append the next element of a to b and maintain the dot product invariant.
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      // After the append, ensure the invariant holds.
      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
      assert AllNonZero(b);
      assert AllBounded(b, 100);
      assert i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0;
    } else {
      // Append the negated previous element of a to b.
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      // After the append, ensure the invariant holds.
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
      assert AllNonZero(b);
      assert AllBounded(b, 100);
      assert i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);
      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int

  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  // Proof by induction on |a|
  // Base case: |a| == 0
  if |a| == 0 {
    assert DotProduct([] + [x], [] + [y]) == x * y;
    assert DotProduct([] + [x], [] + [y]) == DotProduct([], []) + x * y;
    assert DotProduct([], []) == 0;
    assert DotProduct([] + [x], [] + [y]) == 0 + x * y;
    return;
  }
  // Inductive step: |a| > 0
  var a' := a[..|a|-1];
  var b' := b[..|b|-1];
  assert |a'| == |b'|;
  // Apply inductive hypothesis
  assert DotProduct(a' + [x], b' + [y]) == DotProduct(a', b') + x * y;
  // Relate to original sequences
  assert a + [x] == a' + [a[|a|-1], x];
  assert b + [y] == b' + [b[|b|-1], y];
  // Compute dot product
  assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) ==
    DotProduct(a' + [a[|a|-1], x], b' + [b[|b|-1], y]);
  // Expand the dot product
  assert DotProduct(a' + [a[|a|-1], x], b' + [b[|b|-1], y]) ==
    DotProduct(a', b') + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1] + x * y;
  // Use inductive hypothesis
  assert DotProduct(a, b) == DotProduct(a', b') + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1];
  // Combine
  assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      // Append a[i] and a[i+1] to b to preserve dot product
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      // Append -a[i-1] to b to preserve dot product
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
  // After loop, i == |a| and |b| == |a|
  assert |b| == |a|;
  assert AllNonZero(b);
  assert AllBounded(b, 100);
  // Show dot product is zero
  assert DotProduct(a, b) == 0;
}

  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      assert |a[..i]| == |b|; // ensures the precondition for DotProductAppend
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      assert |a[..i]| == |b|; // ensures the precondition for DotProductAppend
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  // After the assertions, we can finish the proof by unfolding definitions
  // of DotProduct for the appended sequences.
  // The proof is trivial but Dafny needs it to see that the invariant holds.
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
    decreases |a| - i
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}
